<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g79166g1205085945824.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>AstroNova Reports Third-Quarter Fiscal 2021 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Bookings of $27.9&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Backlog of $23.2&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue of $28.0&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Operating income of $0.4&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net income of $0.0&nbsp;million, or $0.00 per diluted share </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">EBITDA of $1.7&nbsp;million, or 6.1% of revenue </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>WEST WARWICK, R.I. &#151; December</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;7, 2020 &#151; </B>AstroNova, Inc. (NASDAQ: ALOT), a global leader in data visualization
technologies, today announced financial results for the fiscal 2021 third quarter ended October&nbsp;31, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our Product Identification segment
delivered both revenue and margin improvements in the quarter while Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement continued to reflect the effects of the Boeing 737 MAX grounding and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> on the commercial aerospace
industry,&#148; said Greg Woods, AstroNova&#146;s President and Chief Executive Officer. &#147;Overall performance was aided by continuous improvement initiatives and reduced operating expenses. During the quarter we continued to invest in new
products and technologies to support growth across our businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In Product Identification, strong demand from our TrojanLabel<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, QuickLabel<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> and GetLabels<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">
</SUP>product lines drove <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> and sequential growth in both revenue and operating profit,&#148; Woods said. &#147;Our product and technology innovations are
attracting a broader base of customers to our color label and specialty printing systems. We are helping businesses across a wide spectrum of industries enhance efficiency, eliminate waste and increase brand recognition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In our Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment, growth in our defense business partly offset weakness in commercial aerospace caused by the external
headwinds. Looking ahead, recent progress on the potential approval of multiple coronavirus vaccines, and the FAA&#146;s November decision that cleared the 737 MAX for a return to service, bode well for the T&amp;M segment as we move through fiscal
2022 and beyond,&#148; Woods concluded. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q3 FY 2021 Operating Segment Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Product Identification segment revenue was $22.9&nbsp;million, compared with $21.7&nbsp;million in the prior-year period. Segment operating income was
$3.5&nbsp;million, or 15.4% of revenue, compared with $1.9&nbsp;million, or 8.6% of revenue, in the prior year, reflecting both increased efficiencies and reductions in operating costs. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment revenue was $5.1&nbsp;million, compared with $11.6&nbsp;million in the
same period of fiscal 2020, due to the continued grounding of the Boeing 737 MAX and rapid demand falloff in the aerospace industry related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> The Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment recorded an
operating loss of $0.8&nbsp;million, or negative 14.7% of revenue, compared with segment operating income of $1.4&nbsp;million, or 12.1% of revenue, in the comparable period of fiscal 2020, a direct result of declines in aerospace printer sales and
adverse mix, despite lower manufacturing and operating costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Hardware revenue dropped to $7.7&nbsp;million, compared with $12.2&nbsp;million in the
prior-year period due to Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement weakness. Supplies revenue was $18.0&nbsp;million versus $17.7&nbsp;million in the same period of fiscal 2020. Service/other revenue was $2.4&nbsp;million, compared with $3.5&nbsp;million a year
earlier. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q3 FY 2021 Results Summary </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue totaled
$28.0&nbsp;million, compared with $33.3&nbsp;million in the year-earlier period, with a decline in Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement revenue partly offset by higher revenue in the Product Identification segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit was $9.7&nbsp;million, or 34.7% of revenue, compared with $12.3&nbsp;million, or 36.9% of revenue, in the same period of fiscal 2020. The
decrease reflected lower revenue and less favorable product mix in the 2021 period, primarily in the Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating
expenses totaled $9.3&nbsp;million, down 21.4% compared with $11.9&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2020, reflecting the Company&#146;s cost-reduction actions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income was $0.4&nbsp;million in the third quarters of fiscal 2021 and 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other expense included foreign exchange losses resulting from the weaker Euro and Danish Kroner on exposures in those currencies and higher interest expense.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income was $12,000, or $0.00 per share, compared with net income of $0.5&nbsp;million, or $0.06 per diluted share, for the third quarter of fiscal
2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization (EBITDA) were $1.7&nbsp;million, compared with $2.0&nbsp;million in the third
quarter of fiscal 2020. EBITDA is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure explained in greater detail below under &#147;Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measure.&#148; Please refer to the
financial reconciliation table included in this news release for a reconciliation of EBITDA to net income for the fiscal third quarters ended October&nbsp;31, 2020 and November&nbsp;2, 2019. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bookings were $27.9&nbsp;million, compared with $32.6&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Backlog at October&nbsp;31, 2020 was $23.2&nbsp;million versus $20.8&nbsp;million at the end of the fiscal 2020 third quarter. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">AstroNova launched a range of new products that expanded its addressable market beyond label printing at the PACK
EXPO Connects 2020 international packaging tradeshow. These products included the TrojanLabel <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T2-C</FONT> Print and Apply Solution that eliminates intermediate steps in the typical labeling process. Also demonstrated
were <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-line</FONT> barcode verification systems and label finishing systems. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">AstroNova received an exclusive, multi-year commitment from a major North American air carrier to purchase the
Company&#146;s ToughWriter brand of narrow-format flight deck printers for the carrier&#146;s Boeing 737 aircraft. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q3 FY 2021
Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova will discuss its third-quarter fiscal 2021 financial results in an investor conference call at 9:00 a.m. ET today. To
participate on the conference call, please dial (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">367-2403</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (334) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">777-6978</FONT> (International) approximately 10 minutes prior to the start time and
enter confirmation code 2309769. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You can hear a replay of the conference call from 12:00 p.m. ET Monday, December&nbsp;7, 2020 until 12:00 p.m. ET on
Monday, December&nbsp;14, 2020 by dialing (888) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">203-1112</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (719) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">457-0820</FONT> (International). The passcode is 2309769. A real-time and an archived audio
webcast of the call will be available through the &#147;Investors&#148; section of the AstroNova website, https://investors.astronovainc.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Use of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measure </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to financial measures prepared in accordance with generally accepted
accounting principles (GAAP), this news release contains the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization (EBITDA). AstroNova believes that the inclusion of this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure helps investors gain a meaningful understanding of changes in the Company&#146;s core operating results, and also can help investors who wish to make comparisons between AstroNova and
other companies on both a GAAP and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis. AstroNova&#146;s management uses EBITDA, in addition to GAAP financial measures, as the basis for measuring its core operating performance and comparing
such performance to that of prior periods and to the performance of its competitors. EBITDA also is used by the Company&#146;s management to assist with their financial and operating decision-making. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About AstroNova </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova, Inc. (NASDAQ: ALOT), a global leader in data visualization technologies since 1969, designs, manufactures, distributes, and services a broad range
of products that acquire, store, analyze, and present data in multiple formats. The Product Identification segment offers a complete <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">line-up</FONT> of labeling hardware and supplies, allowing customers to mark,
track, and enhance their products&#146; appearance. The segment is comprised of three business units: QuickLabel<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, the industry leader in tabletop digital color label printing; TrojanLabel<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, an innovative leader for professional label presses; and GetLabels<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP>, the premier supplier of label materials, inks, toners, ribbons, and
adhesives, all compatible with the major printer brands. Supported by AstroNova&#146;s customer application experts and technology leadership in printing, material science, and high-speed data processing, customers benefit from an optimized,
&#147;total solution&#148; approach. The Test and Measurement segment includes the AstroNova Aerospace business unit, which designs and manufactures flight deck printers, networking hardware, and related accessories serving the world&#146;s
aerospace and defense industries with proven advanced airborne technology solutions for the cockpit and the cabin; and the Test and Measurement business unit, which offers a suite of products and services that acquire, record, and analyze electronic
signal data from local and networked sensors. AstroNova is a member of the Russell Microcap<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Index and the LD Micro Index (INDEXNYSEGIS: LDMICRO). Additional information is available by
visiting&nbsp;<U>www.astronovainc.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Information included in this news release may contain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
